msg:To be honest, if this hotel is not located in Yizhuang, but in the suburbs of Beijing, it must have been popular for a long time. Although it is not as high-end as the one in the middle of the bay, it is definitely not worse than Minmetals Narada.
However, he is in a development zone, and there are no tourist attractions nearby, nor is it next to the train station or airport. People in the urban area feel that they are not out of Beijing, and people from other places feel that it is not Beijing, so the positioning has always been awkward. Transformation from a business hotel Parent-child hotels, it can be seen that they have worked hard in the past few years, but they are still not very popular. The reason why we chose this place again is because there are few people and it is clean and fun.
The hotel focuses on the parent-child brand, and the experience of bringing a baby to live is really good.
When I arrived at the store, I gave my baby a small gift, a bunch of snacks in a princess gift box, two bottles of soda water and two cold brewed teas. There is a welcome message on the TV screen when entering the room, and there is a lot of food in the mini bar in the room, all of which are free. There are Perrier, soda, juice, beer, and a bag of dried fruit. In the evening, two cans of the hotel's homemade yogurt were delivered, which were thick and delicious. The fruit was delivered early the next morning. The fruit inside was fresh and of good quality. After checking out of the store, there is also a souvenir, which is a small toy. Anyway, I feel that the whole process is feeding and pleasing the baby~~~
It is said that the hotel has two children's clubs, one is charged and the other is free (it is said that because I didn't go to the free one, this time I bought a hotel package to bring my baby to play, the charged one is included in the package, time (Limited, only paid ones) It is said that the free ones are more suitable for young children. There is a large-screen ocean ball interactive and role-playing area, as long as you stay in the hotel, you can play for free. For this fee, you must buy a hotel package to go, or buy a park ticket alone. There are large-scale climbing castles, two right-angle large slides, a small rock climbing, a small high-altitude expansion project, and two simulators (one helicopter and one car) ), rock climbing and expansion are assisted by staff (need to bring a safety harness), and it is not a big problem for four or five-year-old children to play in it for two or three hours.
There is also a hot spring water park in the hotel package. If you only stay in the hotel, this water park is charged, but the swimming pool is free (there are also two small hot spring pools in the swimming pool, which children can play in). We went to both the water park and the swimming pool. The water park was slightly more crowded, but there were no more than ten families [laughing and crying]. We went to the swimming pool at night and almost no one was there. The water park is open from ten in the morning to eight in the evening, and the swimming pool is open until ten or eleven in the evening. I think the water park is very nice~~ The place is not too big, there are two areas, one is a water play area, there are water slides, water swings and so on, and several large swimming circles (flamingos, dragons and tanks) are free to use, you can It is used to take pictures, and the other area is a bit like a water game like Zhiyong Da Chongguan. Anyway, my baby fell and drank a few sips of water [cover face]. Generally speaking, the water temperature is acceptable. It is very warm inside on May Day, and the Dachongguan area feels a little cold. The water quality is relatively good, very clean, I feel it is due to the lack of people.
The hotel's buffet breakfast is very, very good, and I feel it is better than 80% of five-star hotels at the same price. First of all, there is steak for breakfast, which is deeply in my heart. I like meat. Secondly, all drinks in the bar are free, but they cannot be taken away, and there are still many types. Third, there are too many types of bread and pastries, each of which looks very attractive. Although I only eat whole wheat bread, the children really enjoy it. Fourth, there are very complete types of cheese. My family is full of cheese lovers, so I eat a lot.
Finally, the room is of a suitable size and satisfactory, the toiletries are ok, the smart toilet, the coffee machine is good, and the tea bags and capsule coffee are complete. The disadvantage is that the smart toilet cannot be equipped with a child's toilet seat. Although the hotel provides a small toilet for children, the cleaning is not in place, and it is still not as hygienic as the toilet seat.
